lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme: Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	Lift the patient onto your hands, and have the assistant press the belly while pushing the water towards the lowest part of the back, then take a spatula-shaped trocar like this: It should be cutting on both sides, pointed at the end, but not so sharp that it can reach the intestines when inserted, nor cut them.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude .iij. dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude .iij. dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	Then look to see if the dropsy is invading towards the intestines: you should make your incision about three fingers' width directly below the spine; and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, make your incision to the left of this mark; if it's due to mucus, make it on the right side. Make sure that the patient does not lie on the incision so that the superfluities do not flow into that weak area
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme: Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz .i. petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, .iij. pertus; et .ij. d’autre part, et .i. d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	Then pierce the skin with the trocar and insert it, then move your hand along the trocar between the skin and the fascia as when cutting open a boil to the depth of one finger or less all around. Then pierce the fascia until the trocar reaches the empty space, which is where the water collects. Then remove the trocar and insert this instrument: It resembles a thin silver tube and is made of bronze or light iron, with a small hole at the bottom end and three holes on one side and two on the other. The cutting edge is shaped like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that writers use to cut a feather.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	At the top end of this is the funnel-shaped opening, so that when the instrument reaches the water, you can now tip it up. Remove about half or a third of the water, but not too much at once because if you remove too much too soon, the patient might die from sudden loss of spirit, faint, or approach death
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	but remove according to the patient's strength and disposition of their spirit, and pulse. Then remove the instrument and retain the water, which is now held back by the heart that stops up the hole above the fascia that you pierced earlier. Then begin again with the instrument on another day if the patient can tolerate it, and remove a small amount of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	**fai ce aucun jor:**
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the swelling of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Never are children born who do not have an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place. If this happens, it must be pierced at once with one spatumile made very thin according to this shape: then put one thin lead plug into the hole and tie it and hold it for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and let him urinate, and then replace it. And perhaps there is no need for this at all, because the urine that comes out will not leave the opening closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those whose opening is small are treated with a lead plug, as we have said, and it will widen. Those who do not have the opening in its proper place are blinded, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating unless they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the marrow, and this is a serious condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	The method of treatment is for the patient to lie on his back, then extend the head of the penis and the glans as well, so that the opening falls in the middle, as it should; and guard against loss of blood which often occurs there, and if any occurs, stop the bleeding with whatever stops bleeding, and dress the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	sores on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times these sores appear on the penis, which are an ugly appearance of flesh; and there are malignant ones and non-malignant ones. It is necessary to grasp them with a fine pair of forceps, cut and clean them all, then place moistened cotton in Egyptian ointment; then treat with diaphoretic ointment until they are healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere. Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the sore is malignant, of foul color and putrid, it is necessary to bring cautery. When you have cut it, and if the sore is at the end of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, it is necessary to remove the sore that is inside first; and when it is healed, then treat what remains outside. For when you treat them together, it is not certain that the tip of the penis will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption come into its root and in coition; therefore, cut away everything that is black and corrupt, then apply to the wound a plaster made of honey and flour mixed with the rind of pomegranates and figs, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme: Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And if bleeding occurs, bring the lunar cautery in this manner: This cautery helps with two conditions at once, namely bleeding and corruption; and if the tip of the penis is corrupted and retracted, it is necessary to insert a tin tube into the urethra of the penis and for the patient to urinate through it; and when the skin around the head of the penis that needs to be removed has been hardened, which occurs in those who have not been circumcised or where there is a wound or an abscess, then cut with a sharp instrument until the ligaments are loosened and the tip of the penis is released from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	And if it is difficult to separate them, then cut with a spatula some of the flesh from the tip of the penis and skin; then carefully open between two and place a fine linen cloth moistened in cold water so that it does not harden again.
de la circoncision	de la circoncision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not the same kind of wound that keeps growing like others; nevertheless, when we perform this operation willingly and especially on children, it is necessary to do our best work and make it as easy and safe as possible.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice the circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired by experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who perform circumcision around the age of one day, and even adults, and there is often confusion because there are two layers of skin, and sometimes one is cut instead of the other.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Now the bone comes into contact, and there is double pain; during cleansing, it is not certain that the point of the limb will be secure; and during cleansing of the nail, sometimes the iron escapes, wounds the work, and often times they are born in such a way that they do not require cleansing, as I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	As for the cleansing that is done with force on all the length of the thread, I have found its goodness through experimentation, for it cuts evenly both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	For when you press your hand, it cuts evenly in one single stretch of time; but ensure that the thread is well wrapped around the leather; and the manner of the first operation should be such that you make the child understand, if he hears, that you are only tying the thread around the stick, and then you can let him try all the other ways.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien; et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	Then make him stand upright between your hands and hide the forceps under your feet so that the child does not see them or any of the tools; then put your hand on the stick and blow into it, and draw it up until the skin of the stick is inside; then cleanse it well from the dirt that has gathered there, then tie a double thread knot around it, then tie another knot further down with one or two knots; hold it with both hands by the second knot between the thumb and index finger, and cut between the two knots, then quickly raise your hand and pull the top of the stick.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let the blood flow little by little, for it is nourishing; then apply powder and over the powder a cloth glued with half of a cooked egg yolk tempered with rose water, melted with good fresh rose oil, and leave it overnight until the next day, and cure it again until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the forceps used for cleansing is as follows: The two tips should be thin and sharp, and the tips should be as large as the middle finger equally.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	The error of cleansing is when the heart is inside the incision; therefore it is necessary to extend it with your fingernail before the wound becomes inflamed; and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then use forceps to hold it and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it is more than three days and the part below the stick is swollen, then leave it until the inflammation has subsided, and gently scrape it off; cut it as much as you can move it, and be careful not to damage the skin of the stick, it will not harm it at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat the wound of sudden injury with powders, as we have said when discussing powders; and if you cut too much from the heart and it goes upwards, it will not harm at all; therefore treat it as we have said until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	On the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to obstruction by stone, or congealed blood, or bowel, or dead flesh, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the section on divisions;
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And if the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained due to a stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient must bend over on their knees; place their feet on their back, extend their belly from the part above their back, and have the patient push down as much as they can; thus, the neck of the bladder will be forced open from above, causing the urine to flow out.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And if it does not come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer an extraction using the instrument called "syringe", of which this is the form: it should be made of thin, light silver, like a bird's feather; it should be about one-and-a-half palms long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And the manner of administering the urine is thus: take one doubled thread, and tie a wad of wool or cotton at its end, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe. Remove any excess wool, then lubricate the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, have the patient sit on a chair, raise their bladder and penis, and lubricate them with warm water, olive oil, and egg white.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then fold the penis upwards towards the belly. Insert the syringe further until it reaches the bladder, and have the patient feel when the syringe is empty. If this is not done correctly, it may be because the tube is twisted. Then pull out the thread along with the wad of wool, and the urine will follow the wool. Finally, remove the syringe and allow the urine to flow freely.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and continue using the syringe until the bladder is completely emptied, and then relieve the patient.
des maladies de la vessie	bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When urine or blood enters the bladder and decay accumulates there, and you see water and medicine being distilled out of it, do this with all the instrument called "clepsydra," and its shape is:
Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d’une part, et .i. d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	She is closed and has three openings: two on one side, and one on the other, as you see; and the raised places are such that the medicine cup fits well and plugs the tube without addition, so that moisture can be drawn out, and introduced when necessary.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	And when you see your medicines flowing into the bladder, put the head of the funnel into the moisture and draw out what is inside it. You will then draw the moisture into the catheter, and then push it back in firmly. The moisture will then enter and reach the bladder so that the patient feels it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	"And this is the form of the thin enema used to administer an enema for the bladder."
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	"And it is made of silver or bronze, and the tube is higher up; and below there is one or two small openings where the liquid falls out. Then take a lamb's bladder and put in it the moisture with which you wish to administer an enema to the bladder. Then tie it between the two breasts formed from a doubled thread, and heat one pot of that moisture over the fire. Then insert the tip of the enema into the urethra, then squeeze your hand on the bladder until all the moisture has flowed in."
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	"And if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment and make a circle from it, and pierce it evenly around. Then insert a strong thread into these holes, then assemble the circle like one would assemble a funnel, and put inside what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument. And do as you have done with the bladder, by squeezing your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder."
de la piere	"from the stone"
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	"We have already spoken in the division about the ways of treating stones and removing them with medicines. And we have explained the difference between stones that enter the kidneys and all their signs, and in which stones one should operate by cutting. And in the bladder and in the urethra, and I will tell you clearly and briefly."
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	"I say that stones which enter the bladder occur more often in children. This is a sign that urine leaves the bladder like water in its subtlety. And it appears harsh, and the patient grates his urethra, and he pants many times, and then becomes rigid. And the foundation of this comes from many causes. And the cure for children is easy until they are four years old, but it is very difficult in older people, and it is moderate in young adults, those who are between youth and old age. And the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones."
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines. Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	"And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema in order to remove all the feces that are in the intestines. For sometimes it hinders seeking out the stone."
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche ded ens;	"Then take the patient by the feet and lift them up and move him downwards so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from above. Then have him sit between your hands prepared in such a way that his hands are below his thighs, so that the bladder is entirely inclined downward; then search for it and touch it inside."
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere. Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	"If you feel the stone in space, then hurry now to cut on the stone. And if it does not fall out when touched, then moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand if the patient is a child, or your middle finger if the patient is an adult; and insert it into the stone's foundation and search for the stone, and when you feel it under your finger, guide it to the neck of the bladder. Then press on your finger and push the stone out where you wish to cut it."
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	"And command the assistant to press the bladder with his hand. And tell him to stretch out the thighs upwards with his right hand and remove the skin that is under the thighs in the part where you are cutting with his left hand. Then insert the spatula thus shaped:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	"And cut between what is between the thighs and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the anus. And let it be straight over the stone, with your two fingers always at the bottom, and make the cut across so that it is wide on the outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;"
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	By chance the pressure is so great on the stone that is at its foundation that it bursts forth without effort; and know that there are such stones where there are angles and edges: they are difficult to pass; and there are those that are round underneath, like a globe, from which the exit is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	Therefore, at those where there are angles and edges, make the cut larger; and if it does not work, then you must use pincers that are also like a chisel at the head to extract the stone so that it does not escape; or put underneath one subtle tool curved at the head; and if you cannot manage it thus, then widen a little bit around the hole, and if the skin is cut, then coat it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors. Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie. Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	And if there are multiple stones, first put the largest one at the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then draw it forth, and then remove the smaller ones afterwards if there are more. And if they are very large, then it is necessary to make a larger incision. For two things happen to the patient: either he dies, or the urine comes out immediately where the wound cannot be closed; but in any case, try to draw it out piece by piece with pincers until you have removed them all.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	And once you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, then bind it up, and put on top a cloth dampened in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water to cool the inflamed abscess; then cover the patient's neck and do not untie the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you do untie it, wash the wound very well with oil and water, then dress it with balsam of Joppa and balsam of Basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	And if hot abscesses come in the wound and corrosions, and congealed blood in the bladder causes retention of urine that is known by this way: put your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder and harm it
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	Then wash the wound with water and pitch and salt, and assist the patient in every way that you know until he is healed. And it is necessary that at every dressing of the wound, you bind his two thighs together and gather the dressings onto the wound.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small and it is in the urethra and stuck there so that urine cannot pass, then treat it as I said earlier: cut it many times until you are relieved of this condition, or else excise it from the urethra with this treatment. I have already proven this method.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron rod according to this shape and having three prongs forged into one piece of charcoal:
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then take one thread and bind it around the stalk beneath the stone so that it cannot move backwards into the bladder; then insert the probe lightly into the stalk until it reaches the stone; and twist the probe in your hand against the stone gently, until you can pierce the stone from the other side; then urine will soon flow, then press your hand upon what remains of the stone within the stalk. Thus is it soon broken, and spills out with the urine, and the patient is healed
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you are unable to do this for any reason, then tie one thread beneath the stone and another above it; then make an incision in the stalk at the point of the stone between the two threads; then extract the stone, untie the threads, and cleanse the blood that has congealed in the wound; and care for the patient until he is healed.
de la piere des femmes	Of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in women, and if it does happen, its treatment is difficult, and it is forbidden for three reasons: the first is that by chance the woman may be a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a woman well-skilled who exposes herself to physicians, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	And the third reason is that one might not find a skilled woman in this art of hands; and the fourth reason is that the stone of the woman is more deeply lodged than the stone of man, for which reason it requires a deeper incision, and there is greater fear involved.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if you must perform this operation, then it is necessary for you to find a skilled midwife, and they are rarely found, and if you cannot find one, then seek out a chaste, subtle physician; and present her with a wise maiden who knows the lives of women, or a woman who knows some part of the art, and command her to perform whatever you command regarding the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and examine very carefully if the woman is virgin: then she should place her thumb on the fundament and seek the stone; and if she finds it, she should press it down with her thumb, and instruct her to insert her thumb into the patient's anus, and press her left hand firmly upon the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, she must move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder to below until it reaches the root of the thigh; then cut upon the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the anus where it is usually located and felt by the stone in that part. And do not move your thumb above or below the stone, making the first cut small
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	then insert the knife into the cut if you feel that the stone is close enough to the wound so that it can exit safely; and know that there are many kinds of stones: some small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with roots. Know their appearances to recognize the exit point
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if the blood is too profuse, then apply powdered vitriol and let it remain there for an hour until the bleeding stops. Then return to your work until the stone is removed. And have with you the instruments that I told you about in extracting the stone from men to help you in this task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood is too profuse and it comes from an artery that has been cut, then apply powder to the spot and compress with lint and bandages, but do not resume cutting again, and leave the stone alone without trying to remove it, for fear that the patient may die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And once the heat of the blood is subdued and the spot is healed, then return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	Herne carnose
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Aquous hernia is nothing other than a gathering of moisture or white fat which is underneath the heart of the testicles, containing the egg; and it is called "fat" and sometimes thought to be another egg if it is properly in the membrane of the egg. It is the skin of the testicle between this white fat that we have spoken of, and there would not be any unless it protruded
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this hernia occurs due to weakness in the testicles, with the matter being spread out and expanding
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And sometimes it occurs due to injury to the testicles, and this moisture can have many different colors: it may appear yellowish, red, black, or white. And there are more cases than these;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this gathering: if it is the white fat that we have spoken of, then the swelling will be round, about one inch long like an egg shape, and it will not expose the testicle because it has moisture all around it
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in its own membrane, then the swelling will be round with part of the egg visible, which leads people to believe that it is another egg
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin of the testicle and the white fat, it can be felt quite well. Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, use a square-tipped instrument like the one shown earlier to express it
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Therefore, based on what comes out after using the instrument, you can make a judgment about what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we operate on it using an iron instrument, it is necessary that the patient be fasting according to their strength and the fullness of their body. Then have them lie on their back on something slightly elevated, and place many cloths underneath them
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on the patient's left side, and have the assistant sit on the right side. Have them extend the penis towards one of the two groins on either side of the testicle;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the sharp bistoury and cut through the skin of the testicle along the length up to near the pubic hair, making a straight incision that divides the skin until it reaches the white fat. Carefully scratch away the fat according to your skill;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Then pierce the fat with a large needle and draw out all the water. Then place your forceps and extend the fat upwards. Do not touch the testicle itself but only the fat. Carefully cut away the fat on either side of it, piece by piece, so that if you do not cut it finely enough, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the egg protrudes during your operation, push it back into place once you have finished working on the fat. Then sew up the two layers of skin around the testicle with stitches, and dress the wound like any other.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find that the egg is corrupted by some other disease, it will be necessary to ligate the blood vessels that suspend it in order to prevent bleeding. Then cut away the testicle along with its suspensory ligament and remove the egg entirely, dressing the wound as we have described.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if there is a gathering of water in two places at once, know that these are two hernias. Operate on the second one just like you did the first one, then stop the bleeding and place a compress made of linen moistened with rose oil into the wound
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	Then place another compress made of linen moistened with wine and oil over the two testicles, cover it with doubled cloths, and bind it all together according to this pattern;
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two cloths and stuff them with wool waste according to this shape, sewing them together at the waistband of the breeches. One piece should fit over the buttocks up to the back, while the other fits at the pubic area. The other two ends should be brought together over the two thighs, and the entire binder should be secured in a loop around the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	Sometimes this hernia is treated with a cautery instead of an iron instrument, as follows: Take a sharp cautery needle and burn the skin of the testicle until it becomes inflamed and the white fat that contains the water is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take a cautery needle like this one and pierce through the fat with forceps. Carefully burn away the fat with this hot cautery needle;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	Make the incision in any way that you can, until all the fat is removed. Be careful not to let the fire touch the egg. Know that this procedure is safer than cutting with an iron instrument, and be cautious about bleeding during the operation
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything goes wrong during the procedure, such as a burn, bleeding, or some other complication, treat it according to what has been described earlier
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patient is fearful and unwilling to undergo this operation due to its unpleasantness, you can perform a puncture instead, as follows:
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	Sit the patient on one raised seat; then pierce the abscess at its lower part with a wide spatula, and insert the perforation deeply into the body's length; ensure the hole is large enough for all water to flow freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the location and tie it, allowing the rest of the water to drain, then heal it until the wound is clean.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the white cloth does not allow water to exit through the mouth of the wound, you must insert a pen or the tool used to treat hydrocele water; its shape is shown above. Then enlarge the wound slightly and wait until the water returns and collects again after about six months or so. Once it has collected as before, the patient will recover.
de l’aposteme des coions	Abscess of the groin
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the division of this branch there are several possibilities. Therefore, it seems to me that it is best left alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you the treatment and similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say therefore that many abscesses occur on the body, especially in the groin area; this happens quite often.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	Know this: it is due to excessive acidity and bitterness, which spread to the joints, caused by percussion.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and the color of the boil is similar to that of the body's skin; and it does not cause pain, but is a severe boil.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there are boils that are hard and rough, with dark coloring, which may also come from an artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to an artery, it is recognizable by the arrangement of hot boils that you can feel with your two fingers when you press them.
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it should not be touched at all
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	That which is caused by swelling of the vein is recognizable by its arrangement when touched with two fingers,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	"One can indeed perform a cautery on this type of wound, as well as others."
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	"And then you cut the cord of the birthing canal, and the egg is placed on high, and the tail feathers are white like snow, and free the suspender from all around the egg."
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	"If the egg is already hard-boiled with these characters born, then you should crack the egg and peel it."
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	"And if it is air on the surface or inside the vessels, you should remove all that matter and cut it round."
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	"And if the birth of the flesh is behind the joint, then you should cut all of it and extract the egg, as we have said."
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And when your work is complete, dress the wound with oil and wine-soaked wool, then apply other dressings until it is healed."
de l’aposteme des coions	"wound of the birthing canal"
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	"This is a wound wrapped in a wrapping resembling a boil, with softening of the birthing canal,"
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	"And the patient cries out when it goes away;"
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	"The treatment for this disease is equally fearful as the one mentioned before,"
et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	"Nevertheless, we will tell you how to treat it according to what the ancients did."
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois,	"You should have the patient sit on an elevated seat, then insert the suspender of the birthing canal downward towards your two fingers,"
a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	"up to all the vessels that are near the penis, and hold them firmly, and stretch them out well;"
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert,	"then cut sharply and widely with a scalpel across the surface of the vessels until they are exposed,"
et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	"and then strip from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;"
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	"then insert a needle where there is a doubled thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein appears, and then tie it again at the other end;"
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	"then cut it straight in the middle according to the length of the body, and remove the putrefied membranes;"
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	"then treat the wound like the others where one enters below, so that no vessel empties nourishment into either of the birthing canals;"
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	"for otherwise there will be no harm, but if it comes from all the vessels, then you should tie off both birthing canals at all the vessels;"
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	"so that the testicle does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and it dries up and cannot help itself."
de la routure dou syfac	"on the rupture of the scrotum"
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	"The cause of this rupture is the breaking or stretching of the scrotum towards the abdomen in the area of the groin, causing the intestines to descend from there into one of the birthing canals;"
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	"And this rupture occurs either due to a blow or a fall, jumping, carrying heavy loads, and similar causes;"
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	"The sign of this rupture is that it comes gradually over a long period of time and does not happen suddenly;"
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	"And the swelling is evenly distributed up to its depth because the scrotum presses on the intestines."
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	"And the sign of this rupture is that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there is uneven swelling under the skin near the scrotum, due to the exit of the intestines from the body through the opening in the scrotum."
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	"Sometimes the testicles also descend with the intestines and become trapped there, causing great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed upon."
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	"And in such cases where there is fear of injury from iron, one must avoid using it."
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	"The method for this operation is that you should tell the patient to push the intestines back inside with his hand at the wound if possible;"
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	"then lie him down on a pillow between your hands and lift up his thighs;"
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	"then raise the chest upwards and cut all of the skin off the long part of the scrotum;"
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	"then insert tweezers into the opening of the inguinal canal according to what you need to use them for to open the wound wide enough for the testicle to emerge;"
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	"then strip away the skin of the scrotum that is underneath the skin of the penis until the white fibrous tunic of the scrotum is exposed on all sides;"
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	"then insert your index finger into the space that separates the testicle from the penis, between the white fibrous tunic of the scrotum which is underneath the skin of the testis and the second layer of the scrotum;"
et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	"and separate what is behind the testis and between the second layer of the scrotum. Then use your right hand to push the testis back into the abdominal cavity, lift up the white fibrous tunic with your left hand, and pull the testis towards the inguinal canal along with all of the scrotum;"
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	"and tell the assistant to extend the testis upwards and untie what is behind the ligament;"
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	"and search with both hands to see if any intestine has become wrapped around the white fibrous tunic. If you find any, push it back into the abdominal cavity;"
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	"then take a needle with one thick thread made of ten threads and insert it into the back part of the scrotum which is behind the skin of the penis. Then cut the threads that appear from the needle until there are four threads;"
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	"then tie the threads together in a cross shape using strong sutures of two parts;"
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	"then wrap the threads around themselves and tie them with two knots so that none of the blood vessels that nourish it can enter inside, preventing any swelling from occurring;"
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	"then place the second suture along the first one two fingerbreadths away from it. After these two sutures, leave enough of the scrotum that is underneath the skin of the penis to cover the testicle with one hand;"
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	"then shape the remaining scrotum according to the shape of the testis. Then cut off the part that is under the skin of the penis until the wound is smooth and the belly button appears as we have mentioned earlier;"
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	"then apply moist wool soaked in oil to the wounds and tie the sutures that we have described."
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	"And sometimes it is necessary to cauterize the white fibrous tunic of the scrotum that we have mentioned after the incision, in case of excessive bleeding."
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	"For it often happens that the sutures do not hold, and if they are slow to fall apart, they should be cut with warm water and the treatment that we have described should be applied until they fall apart;"
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	"then treat the wound with other remedies until it is completely healed."
de hernie carnouse	Here's a possible translation of the given Old French text into modern English:
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch of medicine, I never saw anyone daring to treat by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done in the same way as this branch of medicine that is known, tying the vessels together after cutting them slightly below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cut it in half and heal the wound that opens until the vessels bleed out; then treat it as we have said until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	"At times rupture occurs in angles, as we have said, revealing the site; and no part of the intestines descends into the joints, and if any do, it is little, and it repairs hourly."
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	"And yet, if it remains too long in this state, then the wound becomes infected or gangrenous until the intestines descend."
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	"and this happens due to the extension of the gangrene which is at the angles, as we have said, for it becomes extended, then softened and swollen the site and revealed."
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	"And its treatment is by cauterization, as we have previously mentioned; and at times it is treated with iron in this manner:"
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	"And that the patient lies often on their back between your hands, then cut open the site of the rupture swollen with skin according to the quantity of three fingers."
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	"then remove the gangrene that is beneath the skin which succeeds it, then take the iron and place it on the revealed site of the gangrene;"
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	"and press it deeply into the abdomen, then sew up the two exposed sites of the gangrene on top of the iron and sew one and the other."
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	"then remove the head of the iron, and do not cut into the gangrene nor extend the wound further in any way, as I have informed you regarding the treatment of intestinal prolapse."
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	"then treat it by wound care. And when you cut the threads, cleanse and treat the wound until it is healed."
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	"Gangrene is constrained and does not appear in the rupture; cauterization is milder in this site and closer to healing."
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Regarding the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum becomes softened in some men because the tissue inside is softened, and it is unpleasant to see. And it is necessary, when one wants to treat it, that the patient lies on their back and you cut away the softened skin from the natural skin; then bring together the two lips with a stitch, and if you wish, sew first the excess of the softened skin with three or four strong stitches; then cut between the stitches and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Regarding castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Know that castration is forbidden by our law, and it would please me not to speak of it in this book. However, it is necessary for two reasons: one being that the surgeon should know how to respond when asked about it and its treatment; and the other because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats, sheep, pigs, and other beasts. I say therefore that castration is performed in two ways: either by attraction or by incision.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	Hermaphrodites occur in two ways among men: one way is that between the two testicles there opens a cavity resembling the figure of a woman's nature, or it has hair and sometimes urine comes out from it. And the other way among women is that on the thigh there grows both a penis and two testicles. The cure for both males and females is to clean all the wounds together and treat them like other wounds; but for men whose urine flows through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	Of tenaciousness
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tentigene is a hair that grows on the natural part, so ugly to see that some women have it as big as their hand, and this is the treatment. You must remove the excess tentigene with your hand or tweezers, plucking lightly; do not go too deep, lest blood flow, then treat another cure until it is clean; and there is another hair that grows at the mouth of the womb, the anus, and sometimes it may be thicker than usual, and it resembles a cow's appearance, hence the ancients called it «cow disease». You must pluck it, as we have said about tentigene, and treat it until it is clean.
de erratique	Of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	Erratic is when the nature of the woman's womb is not pierced or the opening is small; this can be either congenital or due to illness that has occurred; it may also be due to thick hair growing inside the womb, or a thin and subtle one, and it can be found deep in the womb, on the sides, below, or wherever else it may be. It prevents conception and childbirth, and sometimes causes infertility. Its diagnosis is made by examining the opening of the vagina. If the opening is near the surface, you should examine it with your fingers or a probe. If it is due to thin hair, and is close to two fingers wide, then hurry up and do this: place both index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then press firmly on the two fingers so that the thin hair is rolled up, and placed over the opening. Then take some wool soaked in oil, and apply it to the opening, and let the woman lie down each day until it can no longer be seen. And if the opening is due to thick hair, you should cut it with scissors shaped like a leaf of laurel. If the opening is due to born flesh, then suspend it with tweezers and pluck it out; have some blood-stopping medicines ready, such as aloe, dragon's blood, frankincense, mixed with egg white. Then apply a wide bandage made of lead, so that the wound cannot heal over. Do this for several days, and apply a dry linen compress. Then treat with other remedies until it is clean. And when born flesh comes out in the womb, it should be plucked according to this method, unless it is an infected boil. For one should not touch an infected boil that is in the womb out of fear.
des emorroides	Emorroides are swollen veins that occur around the rectum and anus. They can cause discomfort, pain, and bleeding during bowel movements. Here's how they were described by ancient physicians:
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	**Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement:**
des apostemes de la marris	Of boils of the belly
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.
